<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If we are a PFIC for any taxable year, you will also be deemed to own shares in any of our subsidiaries that are also PFICs in such a year. As
an alternative to the special rules described above, holders of &#147;marketable stock&#148; in a PFIC may elect <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> treatment with respect to their ADSs or
Class&nbsp;B shares. ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares will not be considered marketable stock unless they are regularly traded on a qualified exchange or other market. If the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> election is available and you elect <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> treatment you will, in
general, include as ordinary income each year an amount equal to the increase in value of your ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares for that year (measured at the close of your taxable year) and will generally be allowed a deduction for any decrease in the
value of your ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares for the year but only to the extent of previously included <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> income. In addition, any gain you recognize upon the
sale or other disposition of the ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares will be treated as ordinary income and any loss will be treated as ordinary loss but only to the extent of previously included <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> income. Any loss in excess of previously included <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> income will be treated as a capital loss.
However, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> election would likely be unavailable with respect to your proportionate share in any of our subsidiaries that are PFICs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If you own ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares during any year in which we are a PFIC, you will generally be required to make an annual return on IRS
Form 8621. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Information Reporting and Backup Withholding </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In general, information reporting requirements will apply to dividends paid in respect of ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares and the proceeds received
on the sale or exchange of the ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares within the United States or by a broker with certain United States connections. Backup withholding may apply to payments to you of dividends paid in respect of ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares or
the proceeds of a sale or other disposition of ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares if you fail to provide an accurate taxpayer identification number (certified on IRS Form W&#150;9) or, upon request, to certify that you are not subject to backup withholding
or otherwise to comply with the applicable requirements of the backup withholding rules. The amount of any backup withholding from a payment to you will be allowed as a credit against your United States federal income tax liability, and a refund of
any excess amount withheld under the backup withholding rules may be obtained by filing the appropriate claim for refund with the Internal Revenue Service and furnishing any required information. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Additional Reporting Requirements </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain holders who are individuals may be required to report information relating to an interest in ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares, subject to
certain exceptions (including an exception for ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares held in accounts maintained by certain financial institutions). Holders should consult their tax advisors regarding the effects, if any, of these requirements on their
ownership and disposition of ADSs or Class&nbsp;B shares. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="toc832592_48"></A>F. Dividends and Paying Agents </B></P>

apply to foreign private issuers. Electronic access to these documents may be obtained from the SEC&#146;s website, www.sec.gov, where they are stored in the EDGAR database. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="toc832592_52"></A>ITEM&nbsp;11. QUANTITATIVE AND QUALITATIVE DISCLOSURES ABOUT MARKET RISK </B></P>

Depositary, Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas (&#147;Deutsche Bank&#148;), established October&nbsp;21, 2019 as the record date for payment of annual servicing fees. During 2019, an annual dividend fee of $0.01 was charged per ADS. The
Depositary, Deutsche Bank, established April&nbsp;22, 2019 as the record date for payment of the dividend fee. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Fees and charges payable by ADS

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effective January 2019, Deutsche Bank agreed to pay Ericsson an amount equal to a fixed percentage of the net revenues, if any, collected by it
as a result of charging ADS holders issuance and cancellation fees, and dividend processing and annual servicing fees. In 2019, such amount totaled approximately USD 9.5&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effective January 2019, Deutsche Bank waived the cost of providing the ADS program administrative and reporting services to the extent
provided by Deutsche Bank, and has agreed to bear the cost of certain third-party <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-pocket</FONT></FONT> costs related to the ADS program up to USD 50,000 per year. These costs
include costs for the local custodian&#146;s administration of matters relating to meetings of shareholders and costs of certain transfer agent administration services, such as the registration and transfer of depositary receipts. In 2019, such
amount totaled approximately USD 61,400. </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="toc832592_69"></A><A NAME="toc832592_69"></A>ITEM&nbsp;16C. PRINCIPAL ACCOUNTANT FEES AND
SERVICES </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information set forth under the Section &#147;Financials - Notes to the consolidated financial statements - Note H5
&#150; Fees to auditors&#148; of the 2019 Swedish Annual Report is incorporated herein by reference. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit and Compliance Committee <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> Policies and Procedures </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit and Compliance Committee reviews and approves the
scope of audits to be performed by external and internal auditors and analyzes their results and costs. The Audit and Compliance Committee keeps the Board of Directors informed about the external and internal auditors&#146; performance. It also
makes recommendations to the Nomination Committee regarding the external auditor&#146;s election and fees. In order to ensure the external auditor&#146;s independence, the Audit Committee has established
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> policies and procedures for audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services to be performed by the external auditor. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-approval</FONT>
authority may not be delegated to management. The policies and procedures include a list of prohibited services, and audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services that require
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> by the Committee. Such services fall into two broad categories: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">General <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> &#150; certain services regarding taxes,
transactions, risk management, business improvement, attestation and accounting services and the so called general services (other than prohibited services) have received general <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> by the Audit and
Compliance Committee, provided that the estimated fee for each project does not exceed SEK 1&nbsp;million. The external auditor must advise the Audit and Compliance Committee with a quarterly summary of ongoing projects related to audit and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services and an annual report of fees and expenses for all audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Specific <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> &#150; all other
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services and services subject to general <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> exceeding SEK 1&nbsp;million must receive specific <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval.</FONT>
The external auditor submits an application in writing to the Parent Company for final approval by the Audit and Compliance Committee, including a statement as to whether, in the view of the external auditor, the contemplated services are consistent
with applicable rules on their independence. The Audit and Compliance Committee Chairman has the delegated authority for specific <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> in between Committee meetings, provided that the estimated fee in
each case does not exceed SEK 2.5&nbsp;million. The Chairman reports any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> to the Audit and Compliance Committee at its next meeting. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All services provided in 2019 by the independent auditors were <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> in accordance with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> policies and procedures described above. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="toc832592_70"></A><A NAME="toc832592_70"></A>ITEM&nbsp;16D. EXEMPTIONS FROM THE LISTING STANDARDS FOR AUDIT COMMITTEES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All members of the Audit Committee of a NASDAQ New York-listed company must be independent in accordance with NASDAQ New York and SEC rules.
SEC Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10A-3(b)(1)(iv)(C)</FONT> under the Exchange Act includes a specific exemption from these independence requirements for Audit Committee members of foreign private issuers who are <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-executive</FONT> employee representatives appointed to the Audit Committee pursuant to local law. The Company relies on this exemption and does not consider that such reliance materially adversely affects the ability
of the Audit and Compliance Committee to act independently or to satisfy other SEC requirements applicable to Audit Committees. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="toc832592_71">
</A><A NAME="toc832592_71"></A>ITEM&nbsp;16E. PURCHASES OF EQUITY SECURITIES BY THE ISSUER AND AFFILIATED PURCHASERS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">None. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="toc832592_72"></A><A NAME="toc832592_72"></A>ITEM&nbsp;16F. CHANGE IN REGISTRANT&#146;S CERTIFYING ACCOUNTANT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Nomination Committee, which is comprised of the Chair of the Board of Directors and representatives of Ericsson&#146;s largest shareholders by voting
power, is responsible for proposing the external auditor for election by the shareholders, upon recommendation from the Audit and Compliance Committee of the Board of Directors. Under applicable auditor rotation rules, Ericsson must change auditors
from its current auditor PricewaterhouseCoopers AB (&#147;PwC&#148;) no later than in 2021. In light of the foregoing and to secure timely auditor relation, in 2018, Ericsson initiated a tendering process, overseen by the Audit and Compliance
Committee, for appointment of the Group&#146;s auditor for the financial year 2020 to be elected by the shareholders at the 2020 Annual General Meeting of shareholders (&#147;AGM&#148;). Based on the results of this tendering process, the Audit and
Compliance Committee recommend the Nomination Committee to propose that Deloitte AB be elected new auditor at the 2020 Annual General Meeting. The Nomination Committee&#146;s proposal to elect Deloitte AB as new auditor, was made public by the
Company on February&nbsp;21, 2020. If Deloitte AB is elected new auditor at the AGM 2020, PwC will resign as auditors at the end of the AGM 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In
respect of fiscal years 2018 and 2019 and the subsequent interim period through March&nbsp;19, 2020: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">PwC has not issued any report on Ericsson&#146;s consolidated financial statements or on the effectiveness of
Ericsson&#146;s internal control over financial reporting that contained an adverse opinion or a disclaimer of opinion. The relevant PwC auditor&#146;s reports were not qualified or modified as to uncertainty, audit scope or accounting principles.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">there has not been any disagreement with PwC on any matter of accounting principles or practices, financial
statement disclosure, or auditing scope or procedure, which disagreement, if not resolved to PwC&#146;s satisfaction, would have caused PwC to make reference to the subject matter of the disagreement in connection with its auditor&#146;s reports, or
any reportable event as described in Item 16F(a)(1)(v) of Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F.</FONT> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson has provided PwC
with a copy of the foregoing disclosure and has requested that they furnish it with a letter addressed to the US Securities and Exchange Commission stating whether it agrees with such disclosure and, if not, stating the respects in which it does not
agree. A copy of PwC&#146;s letter dated March&nbsp;
19, 2020, in which they stated that they agree with such disclosure, is filed as Exhibit 16.1. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="toc832592_73"></A><A NAME="toc832592_73"></A>ITEM&nbsp;16G.
 CORPORATE GOVERNANCE </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson, as a company whose shares are listed on NASDAQ New York, is subject to the listing requirements and
certain of the corporate governance requirements of NASDAQ New York and to certain rules of the SEC. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under NASDAQ New York rules, all
members of the audit committee of a NASDAQ New York- listed company must be independent in accordance with SEC rules. SEC rules include a specific exemption from these independence requirements for an employee of a foreign private issuer who is not
an executive officer if the employee is elected or named to the board of directors or audit committee pursuant to the issuer&#146;s governing law or documents, or other home country legal or listing requirements<B>. </B>The Company relies on this
exemption and does not consider that such reliance materially adversely affects the ability of the Audit and Compliance Committee to act independently or to satisfy other SEC requirements applicable to audit committees. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under NASDAQ New York rules, Ericsson is permitted to follow home country practices in lieu of certain NASDAQ corporate governance
requirements that would apply to US companies listed on NASDAQ New York. The rules require disclosures regarding the ways in which Ericsson&#146;s corporate governance practices differ from those required of US companies under the rules of NASDAQ
New York. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These differences include the following: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Employee representatives are appointed to Ericsson&#146;s Board of Directors and serve on Committees (including
the Audit and Compliance Committee and the Remuneration Committee) in accordance with Swedish law. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Employee representatives on the Ericsson Board and committees may attend all meetings of the Board and committees
on which they serve (including those of the Audit and Compliance Committee and the Remuneration Committee) in accordance with Swedish law. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">In accordance with Swedish market practices, the Nomination Committee is not fully comprised of Board members. In
addition to the Chair of the Board, representatives of the four largest shareholders are members of the current Nomination Committee of Ericsson. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">20 </P>
